# 《中国植物志》植物中文正式名读音的统一

<p><span style="font-size: 14px;">（井井只是改了改格式2333）<br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">原文名为《&lt;中国植物志&gt;植物中文普通名的订正和读音的统一》，知网链接已于文末给出。</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">文章发布前已获得作者刘夙老师的授权。</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">全文目录如下：</span><br  /></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">一、改重名</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">二、和种下等级有关的中文名订正</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1. 种和自动名中文名不匹配的订正：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2.由种下等级旧命名法所得中文名的订正：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">三、正字</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1.改掉少数民族的旧称：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2.改掉部分 GBK 字库中未收录的冷僻字：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 3.异体字的订正：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 4.别字的订正：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">四、读音的统一</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1.多音字的整理：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2.单音字的准确定音：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 3.科属中文名的普通话白读：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">附：科属中文名中的同音名称&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);"></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;"></span><br  /></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">井井注：</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);"></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">①为更好地区分文中内容，编者已将</span><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 128, 255);">中文正式名用蓝色标出</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">，</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);">学名用绿色标出</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">，<span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 104, 39);">有争议之处及各种观点用黄色标出</span>。<br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">②本文篇幅较长，无法一次全部推出，故分（上）、（下）两篇。本篇为下篇，取目录第四章及附录内容，</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-decoration: underline;">因此本文标题也与原文标题不同</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">。<br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">③原文中有一些小bug，本文以改正，在此不一一指出。<br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">④封面选自</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-decoration: underline;">《康熙字典·亥集下》</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">。<br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">⑤<span style="font-size: 14px;">本文编者对某些字的读音尚存疑，但在此遵从原文</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">，不予修改。</span><br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">⑥<span style="font-size: 14px;">为最大程度上避免学名造成的排版问题，本文字体可能较小，还请见谅。</span></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">正文如下：</span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;"><br  /></span></p><h1 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;"><span style="font-family:宋体;">四、读音的统一</span></h1><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">要实现植物中文名读音的统一（包括普通话读音的统一和方言读音的统一，本文只讨论普通话读音的统一），需要完成以下几步工作：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">第一，植物中文名中多音字的整理；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">第二，单音字的准确定音；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">第三，白读的审订。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">具体说来，多音字的整理显然是中文名读音统一首先要做的工作，它们往往是造成读音混乱的主要原因。知道了植物中文名中有哪些多音字，在以后的拟名中，就可以有意地回避使用这些字的破读音。而且对于计算机检索来说，如果不将多音字的读音弄清楚，就无法实现真正的按音序排列。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">在多音字整理完成之后，下一步自然是单音字的准确定音。当然，这里的单音字，指的是在植物中文名中只有一个读音的字；有的字在整个语言环境中是多音字，但其他的读音并不用于植物中文名，如中有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">zhong4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">二读，在一般语境中都很常见，但在植物中文名中，就只有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这一个读音，这种字也属于这里所说的“单音字”的范畴。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这两步工作完成之后，植物中文名的文读读法就得到了统一。植物中文名的文读读法（一般用普通话读音代表）是它在汉语一切方言中的白读读法（如果存在的话）的基础，有了这个统一的文读读法基础，就可以根据各方言自己的特点，规定某些植物中文名在各方言中的白读读法。普通话是以北京方言为基础的，北京方言的白读非常丰富，所以普通话的白读也很丰富，对植物中文名来说，主要体现在儿化、轻声和部分字音白读这三点上。由于时间精力所限，笔者未能对种中文名的白读进行审订，下文仅对科、属中文名的白读进行了论述。为了行文方便，部分字音白读的问题提前放到“多音字的整理”一段中讨论。</span></p><h2 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;">1.<span style="font-family:宋体;">多音字的整理：</span></h2><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">经整理，《植物志》中文名中共有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">55</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个多音字（壳、爪、芥这三个字属于普通话的文读和白读的区别），占所使用的全部字数的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2.2%</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其中属中文名和种（含种下等级）中文名中都有的有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">20</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个，仅在种中文名中出现的有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">35</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个，下面分别讨论（均按该字的破读音音序排列）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">属中文名和种中文名中都有的多音字（举属中文名以赅该属中种中文名）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这是一个很古老的植物名用字，读音一直比较混乱。《说文解字》只记载它的一个意义是指“鹿藿”，这个意义已经不用于今天的植物名了。它还有另外两个意思，一指</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">悬钩子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rubus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）的一些结多汁、可食的果实的植物，一指</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藨草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Scirpus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）植物，则均用于今天的植物名。《现汉》虽然收录了此字，但只记载了一个读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> biao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，在这个读音下也只记载了“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藨草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这一个义项。因此，“藨草”的藨读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> biao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是没有问题的，但用做“悬钩子”一义的“藨”字，是否也应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> biao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">呢？</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">传统上，这个义项有两读，一为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> biao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（《广韵》为甫娇切，下引反切均出自《广韵》），一为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（普袍切）。从减少字音复杂性、使植物中文名易读的原则考虑，这个义项似乎应该同样读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> biao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，从而使藨成为一个单音字。但是《植物志》悬钩子属中有许多带“泡”字的植物名，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">“空心泡”“插田泡”“大乌泡”“高粱泡”“蛇泡筋”“栽秧泡”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">之类，上文已述，这些“泡”字实际上是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的别字。很显然，在这些俗名来源地的方言中。“藨”和“泡”是同音的，对应的是普通话的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，只不过因为“藨”字过于冷僻，当初记录这些名字的学者一时找不到这个读音的本字，就用“泡”字做了替代。既然“藨”的这个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音在方言中还有一定的生命力，而且如果将藨字规定统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> biao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，则《植物志》收录的这些带“泡”字的植物名在正字之后读音就会发生变化，从而引而混乱，<span style="text-decoration:underline;">最好的解决的方法，当然是承认“藨”字</span></span><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao1</span></span><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音，并用它作为“悬钩子”这个义项的唯一的正读。</span></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这样一来，不仅上述植物名中误写为“泡”字的“藨”字应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其他如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藨寄生属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gleadovia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">列当科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，因寄生在悬钩子属植物根上而得名）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茶藨子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ribes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虎耳草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，部分种结的果实和悬钩子一样多汗、可食）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莛子藨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Triosteum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">忍冬科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，所结红色肉质果实虽不能食，但外貌似悬钩子）中的“藨”，也均应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。因此从涉及类群的数目和使用频率上看，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">实际上才是“藨”字的正读，而藨草的“藨”的读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> biao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是破读。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字作“松柏”的“柏”讲时，读如字，即</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bai3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。但《现汉》还收了它</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">bo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">两个破读。其中，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时仅用于“黄柏”，而这是“黄檗”的异体。读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时则是译音用字，虽然《现汉》仅举了“柏林”一例，但其他如柏拉图（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">Plato</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、库柏（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">Cooper</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）等音译词中的“柏”也都读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柏拉木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Blastus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野牡丹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“柏拉”也是其属名的音译，因此也应该读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，而不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bai3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薄</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字是个入声字，原本只有一个读音，但在普通话中，却发展出了</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">bo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">三个读音，而且意义已经各不混淆了。其</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音专门指“厚薄”的“薄”，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">表示“稀疏”之义，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">bo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">则专门用于“薄荷”一词。因此，《植物志》的植物中文名中，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薄荷属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mentha</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">美国薄荷属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Monarda</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为唇形科）中的“薄”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薄雪火绒草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薄毛茸荚红豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薄毛粗叶榕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薄毛委陵菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”等个别名字中表“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">稀疏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之义的“薄”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其他表“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">厚薄</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">之义的“薄”均读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，“薄”字也就成为《植物志》的植物中文名中唯一一个有三个不同读音的多音字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在植物名中，绝大多数的“藏”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">西藏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的简称，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，唯独在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藏掖花属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">Cnicus</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藏药木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hyptianthera</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藏蕊鸡骨柴</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Elsholtzia fruticosa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f. i<em>nclusa</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（唇形科，即《植物志》上的“鸡骨柴藏蕊变型”）三个名字中表示“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">隐藏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之意，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">cang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。还有一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">武藏山枇杷</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Eriobotrya deflexa </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">f.<em>buisanensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，即《植物志》上的“台湾枇杷武藏山变型”）中的“藏”也读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字在植物名中极常见，绝大多数情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> da4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大黄属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rheum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（蓼科）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。除了这个属的植物外，其他读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> dai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的仅有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大黄橐吾</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ligularia duciformis </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">一个（指其叶子像大黄），而“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大黄檗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大黄药</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大黄柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大黄花堇菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”等名中的“大黄”和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大黄属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">毫无关系，仍读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">da4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">倒</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：大部分情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为形容词，表示“颠倒的”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">之意，但在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">熏倒牛属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Biebersteinia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牻牛儿苗科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">攀倒甑</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Patrinia villosa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">败酱科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）这两个名字中，为动词补语，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：上文已述，这个字有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">gan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">二读，表示“有一定用途的细长的木头或类似的东西”之义时，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">花旗杆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”、“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">旗杆芥</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”二名；表示“器物的像棍子的细长部分”之义时，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">扁担杆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">箭杆风</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">箭杆杨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">酸脚杆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">秤杆树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”等均取这个读音。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">干</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字一般读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，但在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绿干柏</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cupressus arizonica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（柏科）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">直干蓝桉</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eucalyptus maideni</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桃金娘科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，《植物志》误作“直杆蓝桉”）中做“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">树干</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”讲时，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（这时其繁体字为“幹”或“榦”）。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">射干</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Belamcanda</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸢尾科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）的干字，在繁体字中仍作“干”，故只能读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，而不能读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。至于“射”字，古有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> she4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">ye4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">二读，其中</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ye4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是一个十分冷僻的破读音，宜废，只读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">she4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葛</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字作植物名时一般读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ge2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，但在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">诸葛菜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Orychophragmus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ge3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。在作译音用字时，也读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ge3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，所以</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葛萝槭</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Acer grosseri</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槭树科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">锐颖葛氏草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Garnotia acutigluma</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“葛”均读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ge3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">行</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在一般语境中，这个字读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xing2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为读如字，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> hang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">则为破读，但在植物名时，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">hang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的情况和读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xing2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的一样多。所有带地名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">太行</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的植物名如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">太行菊、太行花、太行铁线莲、太行阿魏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，以及</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">二行芥属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Diplotaxis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">单行节肢蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Arthromeris wallichiana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">水龙骨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">单行贯众</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cyrtomium uniseriale</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鳞毛蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">行柑</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Citrus reticulata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> cv.<em>Hanggan </em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中的“行”都读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> hang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xing2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的则有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阴行草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Siphonostegia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">独行菜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lepidium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">平行鳞毛蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dryopteris indusiata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鳞毛蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">留行草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Blastus ernae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野牡丹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">独行千里</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Capparis acutifolia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山柑科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">爬行马先蒿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis reptans</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">匍行狼牙委陵菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Potentilal cryptotaeniae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>radicana</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）这些名字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">壳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字也是入声字，原本只有一个读音，但在普通话中有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qiao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ke2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">两读，前者为文读，后者为白读。显然，若用植物中文名的文读读法，所有的“壳”都应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qiao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。但鉴于“壳”的这两个读音相差太大，而且声母也不相同，把它看成一个多音字也是可以的。带“壳”字的植物名，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">贝壳杉、红厚壳、厚壳桂、厚壳树、壳菜果、山壳骨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，其中的“壳”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字基本都出现在口语中很少使用的复合词（如“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">壳菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）和准复合词（如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">“红壳”“厚壳”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">之类）中，仅“贝壳”在口语中比较常见。植物中文名本身是一套书面语系统，所以口语读音能少用就应少用，鉴此，笔者建议，在属种中文名中，除“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">贝壳杉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的壳读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ke2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">外，其余“壳”字宜一律读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qiao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">此外，蕨类植物还有一个科名叫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蚌壳蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">Dicksoniaceae</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（模式属我国不产）。和“贝壳”类似，其中的“壳”字也以读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ke2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为好。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蚂</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在植物名称中，这个字只出现在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">“蚂蝗”“蚂蚁”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">“蚂蚱”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这三个原本表示动物的词中。前二者中的蚂读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ma3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，“蚂蚱”的蚂读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ma4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，是不难区分的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒙</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：读如字时，音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">meng2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，作音译字时，音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">meng3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。在植物中文名中，这两个读音都很常见。纯大多数读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">meng3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的场合，“蒙”都作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒙古</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”解，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒙椴、蒙菊、蒙桑</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，或出现在“蒙古”一词中，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒙古韭、蒙古蒿、蒙古葶苈</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，仅一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒙氏马先蒿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Pedicularis monbeigiana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒙</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”是其他专有名词的音译字。读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">meng2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时，意义则比较多样，主要是出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒙自</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（县名，为云南省红河哈尼族彝族自治州首府）和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">乌蒙</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（山名，在云南、贵州交界处）这两个地名中，此外还有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒙蒿子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Anaxagorea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（番荔枝科）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">密蒙花</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Buddleja officinalis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马钱科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">罗蒙常山</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Dichroa yaoshanensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虎耳草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒙山附地菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Trigonotis tenera</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）四名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：上文第三节“正字”中“异体字的订正”一段中已述，这个字有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">pao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">二音，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时意为“虚而松软，不坚硬”，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">泡桐属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">泡滑竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">泡沙参</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时意为“泡沫”“像泡沫的”。植物中文名中表示“鼓起的中空物”之义的“泡”，笔者在上文已建议作为“脬”的异体字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：除在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荸荠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（口语中常念轻声）外，其余场合均念</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ji4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">尿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字在植物中文名中一共只出现</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">次，在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马尿藤</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Campylotropis bonatiana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">尿罐草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Corydalis moupinensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">罂粟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">niao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，但在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马尿脬属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Przewalskia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马尿脬</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">P. tangutica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中则读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sui1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字在植物中文名一共只出现</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">8</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">次，但其中却有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个属名。这</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">7</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个名字是：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芫荽属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Coriandrum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芫荽</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> C. sativum</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伞形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山芫荽属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cotula</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山芫荽</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. hemisphaerica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芫荽菊</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. anthemoides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（三者均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">水芫花属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pemphjs</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">水芫花</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">P. acidula</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">千屈菜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芫花</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Daphne genkwa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瑞香科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。前</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">5</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个含“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芫荽</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的名字中的“芫”，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，后</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个含“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芫花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的名字中的“芫”，则读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> yuan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(18)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柚</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字一般作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">橘柚</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的“柚”讲，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> you4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柚木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Tectona</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柚木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">T. grandis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马鞭草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">you2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(19)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">爪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字虽然不是入声字，但在普通话中，也有意义几乎没有差别的文读和白读两个读音，文读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，白读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhua3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。根据上面“壳”字下所述的口语读音尽量少用的处理原则，笔者建议仅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">盐爪爪属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Kalidium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">金爪儿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Lysimachia grammica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">报春花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）这两个口语色彩十分浓厚的名字中的“爪”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhua3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其他名字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹰爪花、爪耳木、大爪草、猫爪藤、假鹰爪、鸡爪草、东爪草、龙爪茅、鹰爪豆、鸡爪簕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，其中的“爪”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">宜均读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(20)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在多数情况下，此字为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">名词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zuan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钻喙兰、钻柱兰、假钻毛蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。但在个别名字中作</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">动词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zuan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，这些名字包括</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钻天柳属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Chosenia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杨柳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钻地风属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Schizophragma</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虎耳草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钻天杨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Populus nigra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小钻杨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">P. </span></em><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#47C1A8;">×</span></em><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> xiaozhuanica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杨柳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）等。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">最后要讨论一下“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”字的读音。这个字原本只有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">一个读音，但普通话吸收了吴方言的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音，遂使之成为有文白二读的多音字。据笔者所知，在植物学界，把此字统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的人是相当多的。但据《现汉》，这个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音仅出现在“杉篙”“杉木”二词中，其他情况下均应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">shan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">那么杉木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cunninghamia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（杉科）的“杉”是否应该读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">呢？《现汉》对“杉木”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">一词的解释是：杉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(shan1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">树的木材。这就是说，只有在指</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cunninghamia lanceolata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这种植物的木材时，“杉木”中的“杉”才读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。但是作为植物名称的“杉木属”和“杉木”两词中的“木”，作“木材”解似不妥，似乎作“树木”解才更合理。比如像灰叶杉木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> C. l.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> cv.<em> Glauca</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和软叶杉木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> C. l. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">cv. <em>Mollifolia</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这两个名字，显然不能理解为“灰叶杉树的木材”或“软叶杉树的木材”。因此，“杉木”在作为植物名称时，“杉”字仍应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">shan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">诚然，我们可以认为“杉木”一名是来源于“杉树的木材”这个本义，而实际上，这种来源的植物名称也确实有不少，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bixa orellana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红木科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蚬木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Excentrodendron hsienmu</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">椴树科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">轻木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ochroma lagopus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木棉科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">铁木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ostrya japonica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桦木科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），其中的“木”本义都是“木材”。但这至多说明，现在“杉木”一词中的“木”作“木材”和“树木”两义讲是都可以说通的。既然如此，何必仅仅为了一个并不是“杉木”的唯一解释的“杉树的木材”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">之义，就在中文植物名中生生保留一个两读音使用频率严重不对称的多音字？</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">因此，恰恰和流行的念法完全相反，<span style="text-decoration:underline;">笔者建议，所有植物中文名中的“杉”，均应统读为</span></span><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shan1</span></span><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅在种名中出现的多音字：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">把</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：多读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ba3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">刀把木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cinnamomum pittosporoides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">樟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">长把马先蒿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis longistipitata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伞把竹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Fargesia utilis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）三名中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ba4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">卜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萝卜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bo</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（轻音），是“蔔”的简化字。但在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">勒加卜蕉</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Musa nagensium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芭蕉科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">拉卜楞杜鹃</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Rhododendron labolengense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名中为音译字，不是“蔔”的简化字，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">埔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：广东东部县名“大埔”中的“埔”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为地名特殊读法（粤方言中“埔”只有这一个读音，但在普通话中，除大埔外的其他地名中的“埔”仍读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如黄埔）。含这一地名的植物名如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大埔杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大埔槭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。在东南亚国名“柬埔寨”中，埔读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> pu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柬埔寨子楝树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柬埔寨草胡椒</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">场</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：杨在植物名中虽仅出现</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">5</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">次，却有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个是破读。常用的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chang3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音仅用于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牧场黄芪</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Astragalus pastorius</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">草场蝇子草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Silene platyphylla</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>praticola</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石竹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。另三个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">土场白头婆</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Eupatorium japonicum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>tozanense</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">龙场梅花草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Parnassia esquirolii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虎耳草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猴场耳蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Polystichum houchangense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鳞毛蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“场”都出现在南方地名中，而南方地名中的“场”多做“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">集市</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”解，这时应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> chang3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">当</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小叶当年枯</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Arctous microphyllus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）一名中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其余情况均读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> dang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">地</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这是植物名称中很常用的一个字，绝大多数情况下都读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">di4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">忽地笑</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lycoris aurea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石蒜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）一名中作形容词的副词化后缀时，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">de</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">轻声。这个读音完全是口语，没有对应的文读。其他没有“地”这个后缀的方言都是按</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">di4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音将这个字转换到自己的语音体系里的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">肚</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：本读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">du4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，但在作“用作食品的动物的胃”解时，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">du3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。符合这一意义的植物中文名有两个，即</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牛叠肚</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rubus crataegifolius</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猪肚木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Canthium horridum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。另有一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鱼肚腩竹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bambusa gibboides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“肚”则因为出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">肚腩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这个复合词中而仍读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">du4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">发</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在植物名中，多数情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> fa4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，意为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">头发</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，仅甜橙的一个品种</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">贾发脐橙</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Citrus sinensis </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">“Jaffa”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芸香科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">发</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”因为是音译字而读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fa1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：多数情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> fei1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为音译字，仅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菲叶猕猴桃</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Actinidia cinerascens</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猕猴桃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“菲”意为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菲薄</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”而读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fei3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芥</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字在普通话中文读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，白读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，且</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">只出现在“芥蓝”“芥菜”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">两词中。其中“芥菜”又是一个多音词，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jie4cai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时指</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brassica juncea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的原变种，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">gai4cai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时仅是</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">B. j. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. <em>foliosa</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为十字花科）这个变种的俗称，而且正写应为“盖菜”。在《植物志》的中文植物名中，芥蓝</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">B. alboglabra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（亦为十字花科）的芥应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，是没有问题的，但“芥菜”一词单用时仅用于</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">B. juncea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的种和原变种，这时应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，至于</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">B. j.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. <em>foliosa</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，《植物志》上叫“大叶芥菜”，这里的“芥菜”并未单用，而且显然是继</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">承自种名，所以读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gai4cai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是不合适的。综上所述，《植物志》中文植物名中，只有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芥蓝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的“芥”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其余均读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莞</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">刺子莞属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhynchospora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“莞”用的是本义，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">guan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，而</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">东莞润楠</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Machilus longipes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">樟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的莞应破读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">guan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，是地名的特殊读音（当然，大部分人对这一破读比对本读熟悉）。东莞为广东市名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">华</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：大部分情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> hua2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">华山</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这个地名中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hua4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。以“华山”为名的植物共有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">11</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个类群，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">华山新麦草、华山野丁香、华山松、华山马鞍树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。华山位于陕西省，为我国名山，又名西岳。但要注意的是，并不是所有“华”和“山”的连用都是“华山”这个地名，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">华山姜、华山楝、华山矾、华山竹、华山蒌</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这五个名字中的“山”字是连后的，“华”单独表示</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">中华</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之意，因此仍读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hua2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">奇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">奇羽鳞毛蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dryopteris sieboldii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鳞毛蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）一名中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ji1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其余情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">间</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">间序豆腐柴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">间序狗尾草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">间断委陵菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄金间碧竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">8</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个名字中，“间”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">做“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">间断</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”解，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jian4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其余情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">降</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字在植物名中一共只出现</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">次，其中</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">降香</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dalbergia odorifera</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）的“降”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jiang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，而</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">降龙草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Hemiboea subcapitata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">密齿降龙草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">H. s. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. <em>denticulata</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">污毛降龙草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">H. s.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. <em>sordidopuberula</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苦苣苔科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）三名中的“降”读</span><span
