style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xiang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枸</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枸头橙</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Citrus aurantium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芸香科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“枸”来自“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枸橼</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，因而应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ju3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，另两个复合词“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枸骨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枸杞</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中的“枸”均应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gou3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">筠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：冷僻字。在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">筠竹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Phyllostachys glauca</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> yun2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">筠连雪胆</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hemsleya pengxianensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jun1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为地名特殊读法。筠连为四川省南部一县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(18)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莨菪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> lang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薯莨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">liang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(19)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">量</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在“无量山”这个地名中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">liang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">无量山铁角蕨、无量山小檗、无量山箭竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。无量山为云南省山脉名。其他情况读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> liang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">量天尺、度量草、小叶度量草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(20)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：也是植物名称中的常用字。大部分情况下读如字，即</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lv4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅在“鸭绿”这个地名中读破为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> lu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸭绿蔷薇、鸭绿乌头、鸭绿薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。鸭绿江为中朝界河。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(21)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">漂</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字在植物名中仅出现</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">次，在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">漂筏薹草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Carex pseudo-curaica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（莎草科）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">piao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，在漂</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">亮风毛菊</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Saussurea bella</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">piao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(22)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">翘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字读如字时，音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qiao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">翘喙马先蒿、翘距虾脊兰、翘首杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。但在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">连翘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这个著名植物名称中读破为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qiao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(23)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苣</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：绝大多数情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ju4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苣荬菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sonchus arvensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(24)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">撒</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字在植物名中也只出现</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">次，在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">撒金碧桃</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Amygdalus persica </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">f.<em>versicolor</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sa3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">撒尔维亚</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Salvia officinalis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）这个音译的植物名中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sa1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(25)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">散：本义是指一种中药制剂名时，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">san3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">铁箍散、赤胫散、通光散、拔毒散</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。作形容词、意为“零散，不集中”时，也读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> san3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅用于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">散毛樱桃</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cerasus patentipila</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">散痂虎耳草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Saxifraga diffusicallosa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虎耳草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。其余情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">san4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(26)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：大部分情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">suo1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎车柽柳</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Tamarix sachuensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柽柳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为地名特殊读法。莎车为新疆县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(27)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">少</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：大部分情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">少年红</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ardisia alyxiaefolia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫金牛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(28)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">缩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：大部分情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> suo1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">缩砂密</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Amomum villosum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">姜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">su4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为中药材名传统读法。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(29)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">台</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：大部分情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（多指“台湾”），仅在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天台</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这个地名中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> tai1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，包括</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天台铁线莲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天台阔叶槭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天台鹅耳枥</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天台小檗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">四名。天台山为浙江中部山名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(30)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">弹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字在植物名中少用，在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">金弹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Fortunella </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">“Chintan”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芸香科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫弹树</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Celtis biondii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、异叶紫弹树</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. b. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em>heterophylla </em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黑弹树</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> C. bungeana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">榆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中做名词，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">弹裂碎米荠</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cardamine impatiens</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">弹刀子菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mazus stachydifolius</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中做动词，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(31)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鲜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：凡出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">朝鲜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这一国名中，均读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xian3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其余读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> xian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(32)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">相</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：出现在地名和人名中时，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xiang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，包括相岭南星</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Arisaema smithii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（天南星科）、大相岭蹄盖蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Athyrium daxianglingense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蹄盖蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">相马石杉</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Huperzia somai</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石杉科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。其中（大）相岭是四川西南部山名，相马为日本人名。其他情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xiang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(33)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">宿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：多数情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> su4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">星宿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中时读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xiu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，包括</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">矮星宿菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lysimachia pumila</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">多育星宿菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> L. prolifera</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">报春花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。与二者同属的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红根草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">L. fortunei</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如为了避重名而改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">星宿菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的话（详见上文第一节“改重名”中的相关论述），其中的“宿”自然也读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xiu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(34)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">椅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字在植物名称中极少见。在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">椅子竹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dendrocalamus bambusoides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）一名中读如字，即</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。但在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">椅杨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Populus wilsonii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">及其变型</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">短柄椅杨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">P. w. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">f.<em> brevipetiolata</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">长果柄椅杨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> P. w. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">f.<em>pedicellata</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杨柳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）三名中，“椅”字的本义是指</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山桐子</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Idesia polycarpa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大风子科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），此处用来拟形，故应按这一义项的破读音，读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(35)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">长</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字在植物名称中极常见，绝大多数情况下读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> chang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">徐长卿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cynanchum paniculatum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萝藦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）一名中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> zhang3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><h2 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;">2.<span style="font-family:宋体;">单音字的准确定音：</span></h2><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">下面列出《植物志》植物中文名中因冷僻而不易读准的单音字，以及读音存在混乱状况、需要讨论厘正的单音字共</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">616</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个（占全部使用字数的四分之一强），按笔画排列（其中有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">11</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个字</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字，暂按其繁体笔画排列，这</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">11</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个字是：紏、穇、薲、簩、繸、蘋、蘡、蘵、欓、虉、圞）。为方便读者作进一步研究，笔者还对一些字义作了解释。本段的写作参考了</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">Artemisia </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">整理的“植物生僻字集”（未发表），特此致谢。为节省篇幅，所举之例不再给出学名和所属科，而且均选自按上述第一至三节所述方法订正后的《植物志》植物名录，遇有和《植物志》实收名称不同时，不再作说明。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">了：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">liao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">了墩黄芪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”、“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">了哥王</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”二名。普通话中“了”作助词时的读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> le</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（轻声）不用于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">儿：在植物中文名的文读读法中，此字统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> er2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，但在普通话白读中，大部分“儿”字是表</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">儿化</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的后缀，详见下文“科属中文名的普通话白读”一段。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">叉：在植物中文名中统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">cha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其他读音都是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">子：在植物中文名的文读读法中，统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，但在普遍话白读中，一部分做为名词后缀的“子”要读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">轻声</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，详见下文“科属中文名的普通话白读”一段。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">什：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，多出现在地名中，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">米什米咖啡、喀什菊、克什米尔蝇子草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。普通话中另有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> shen2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">一音，仅出现在“什么”一词中，不用于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">冈：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> gang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">青冈、井冈山猕猴桃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gang3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">分：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fen1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> fen4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">切：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">切边铁角蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名中的“切”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qie1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">刈：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">三刈叶吴萸</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">匹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">五匹青、匹菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">扎：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阿扎蝇子草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">扎鲁小叶杨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中都读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不读其他音。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">斗：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dou3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蜂斗草、耧斗菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> dou4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">片：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pian4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">长片蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">异片苣苔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">韦：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wei2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瓦韦、石韦</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> wei3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">丕：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">春丕虎耳草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。春丕（谷）为西藏自治区亚东县的旧称。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">乐：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> le4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伯乐树、乐东锥</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yue4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仔：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zai3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">米仔兰、仔榄树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。含这个字的植物名都来自粤方言或闽方言。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(18)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">们：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">men2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">图们黄芩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">图们薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”二名。另一作人称代词复数后缀时的读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> men</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（轻声）不用于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(19)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">凹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">凹舌兰、凹叶瑞香</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一仅在地名用字中出现的读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> wa1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(20)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">刍：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石龙刍、刍雷草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(21)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卡：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ka3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，只出现在地名、人名译音中，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">浪卡子岩黄芪、斯里兰卡天料木、卡开芦</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qia3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(22)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">头：在植物中文名的文读读法中，统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tou2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，但在普通话白读中，一部分做为名词后缀的“头”要读轻声，详见下文“科属中文名的普通话白读”一段。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(23)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">宁：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ning2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">辽宁香茶菜、伊宁风毛菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ning4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(24)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">尔：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">er3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瓶尔小草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名中的“尔”虽然可能是“儿”的别字，但因此名使用甚广，其中“尔”字不宜当成儿化后缀。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(25)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">扒：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ba1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">扒地蜈蚣</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">pa2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(26)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">札：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zha2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">札达黄芪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，札达为西藏县名。其他读音都是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(27)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">术：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苍术、白术、莪术、术叶合耳菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等名。这个读音是该字做植物名时的破读，其本读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> shu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(28)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">正：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zheng4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">正里白、正宇耳蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zheng1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅用于“正月”一词，不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(29)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">穴：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xue2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">岩穴蕨、穴子蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">xue4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(30)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">艽：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jiao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">秦艽</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名。不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jiu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(31)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">亚：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ya4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为普通话统读，其他的读音都是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(32)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">任：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">任豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名因是纪念我国著名教育家任鸿隽，故其中的“任”字读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ren2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">ren4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(33)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">佤：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wa3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">佤箭竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。佤族是我国少数民族之一。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(34)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">兴：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xing1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">宝兴龙胆、兴安杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xing4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(35)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">冲：除“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">冲绳短肠蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”外，这个字只出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">腾冲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这个地名中，二者均读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">chong4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(36)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">吐：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">吐鲁番锦鸡儿、龙吐珠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">tu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(37)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">夹：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">夹竹桃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jia1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jia2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(38)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">孖：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ma1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">孖竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此字是粤方言词，意为“成对，双”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(39)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">曲：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">曲枝天门冬</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">弯曲碎米荠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼠曲草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(40)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">朴：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">po4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">朴树、大叶朴、朴叶楼梯</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">草。这个读音是该字做植物名时的破读，其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(41)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">汗：在“阿富汗”中音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> han4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。有人认为应该读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> han2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，但考</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Afghanistan </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">一词的字源，和作“可汗”简称的“汗”并无关系，因而是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(42)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">百：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bai3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百合、百金花、百山祖冷杉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。广西地名百色的“百”，旧读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，此音今已废。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(43)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">祁：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">祁连圆柏、祁门黄芩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(44)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">纤：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">纤花蒲桃、纤细柽柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qian4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(45)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">肋：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lei4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">三肋果、肋柱花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音都是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(46)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芋：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如海芋、茵芋，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(47)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> xiong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山芎、川芎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(48)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芏：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">du4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茳芏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">短叶茳芏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(49)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芒：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫芒、芒苞草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">wang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(50)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芨：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ji1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芨芨草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名。有的地方植物志上把“白及”写成“白芨”，这种写法是错误的，因此“芨”绝无</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ji2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(51)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">血：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xue4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">血水草、龙血树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。普通话中的白读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">xie3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(52)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">观：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">guan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">观音座莲、鹅观草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> guan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(53)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">那：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">na4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">那坡榕、那藤、错那凤仙花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(54)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">丽：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">li4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">美丽桐、丽薇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> li2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(55)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">乸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">na3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸭乸草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此字是粤方言词，意为“雌，母的”，习惯置于所修饰的名词后面（为古越语语法残留）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(56)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">伯：在植物中文名中只有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这一个读音，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伯乐树、西伯利亚早熟禾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音都是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(57)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">似：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">si4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">相似石韦、似血杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> shi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅见于“似的”一词，不出现在植物中文名中。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(58)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">伽：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伽蓝菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qie2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不读其他任何音。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(59)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">佘：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">she2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">佘山羊奶子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。佘山为上海山名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(60)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">佛：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">佛甲草、佛手、佛氏马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。需要注意的是，“佛”字即使作音译字也仍读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> fo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，而不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> fu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(61)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">刨：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红楠刨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">刨花润楠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”二名。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(62)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">劲：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jing4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">劲直菝葜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">劲枝异药花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jin4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">只出现在普通话口语中。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(63)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">吾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> wu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，只出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">橐吾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(64)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">呐：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> na4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，只出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唢呐草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(65)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">姊：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">七姊妹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jie3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(66)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">尾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wei3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">狗尾草、大尾摇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">只出现在普通话口语中。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(67)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">岐：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">岐山金丝桃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。岐山为陕西县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(68)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">应：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ying4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，只出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">感应草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ying1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(69)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">弄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">long4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瓦弄杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。瓦弄为我国西藏东南部地名。另一更常见的读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> nong4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(70)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">折：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhe2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">折苞风毛菊、急折百蕊草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(71)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">更：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">更里山胡椒</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的“更”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">geng4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> geng1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。更里山为台湾山名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(72)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">杉：上文“多音字的整理”一段中，已述此字在植物中文名中最好统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，否则，“杉木”的杉应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(73)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">杞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枸杞、杞柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(74)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">杧：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杧果</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。俗作“芒果”，非。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(75)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">汶：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wen4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茂汶蟹甲草、汶川柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音都是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(76)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">汾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fen2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">汾河莎草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> fen1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。汾河为山西水名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(77)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">沅：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yuan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">沅陵长蒴苣苔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。沅陵为湖南县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(78)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">沉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chen2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">沉香、沉水樟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。旧多作“沈”，现规定“沈”音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> chen2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时为“沉”的异体字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(79)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">沔：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mian3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">沔县薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。沔县为陕西县名，今作勉县。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(80)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">没：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">没药</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> mei2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为普通话白读，不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(81)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">甫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹤甫碱茅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(82)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">系：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葡系早熟禾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。葡系为该植物地方名，含义不详。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(83)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">羌：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qiang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">羌塘雪兔子、羌活</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(84)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">肖：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xiao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">肖笼鸡、肖竹芋</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为“相似”之意。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xiao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅用于姓氏和音译字，不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(85)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芡：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qian4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芡实</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(86)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芩：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qin2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄芩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(87)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄芪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(88)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芮：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> rui4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石龙芮</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(89)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芷：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">白芷、芷叶前胡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(90)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苁：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">cong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">草苁蓉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”、“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">肉苁蓉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”二名，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> cong2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(91)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苈：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">li4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葶苈</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(92)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苋：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xian4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">反枝苋、马齿苋</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(93)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苎麻、石荠苎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。此字本作“苧”，现已作为“苎”的旧字形，勿误读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">ning2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(94)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苡：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薏苡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(95)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">诃：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">he1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为音译字，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">诃子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(96)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">还：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">huan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">还亮草、还阳参</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> hai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为普通话口语中的副词，不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(97)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">邯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">han2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰邯千金榆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。兰邯（山）为台湾山名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(98)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">酉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">you3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">酉阳楼梯草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。酉阳为重庆市辖自治县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(99)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">钉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ding1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钉头果、白鼓钉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ding4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(100)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">闷：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">闷奶果</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中，意为“密闭，不透气”，故读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">men4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">men1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(101)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">阿：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> a1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，全部为音译字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阿魏、阿尔泰薹草、阿拉伯婆婆纳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">e1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(102)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">陇：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> long3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">陇川秋海棠、陇蜀杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> long2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(103)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">侏：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">侏碱茅，侏儒花楸</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(104)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">兖：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兖州卷柏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(105)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">刹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">刹柴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">青刹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫刹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”三名。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> cha4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅用于“刹那”一词，不用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(106)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">单：在植物中文名中统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。中药材名中有一个“</span><span
