style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">单州漏芦</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，其中的“单”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，单州为山东单县的旧名。这一名字未被《植物志》用作植物正名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(107)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">juan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">卷柏、卷花丹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> juan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(108)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">参：所有植物中文名中的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">参</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”都读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shen1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，本读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> can1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和其他读音如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">cen1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">san1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等都不用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(109)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">咀：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ju3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">咀签</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(110)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和：在植物中文名中统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">he2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(111)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">咖：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">咖啡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ka1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ga1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅用于“咖喱”一词，不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(112)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">坭：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ni2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">坭竹、坭簕竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。此字为粤语地方字，本义同“泥”，常用作地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(113)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">奄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">奄美短肠蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。奄美（大岛）为日本西南部一岛名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(114)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">岷：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">min2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">岷县薹草、岷江柏木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">min3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(115)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">弦：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xian2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">弓弦藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xuan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(116)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">弩：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">nu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">弩刀箭竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">nu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(117)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">怯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">羞怯凤仙花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">羞怯杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”二名，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> que4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(118)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">担：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">一担柴、扁担杆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> dan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(119)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">拉：在植物名中均读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> la1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">喜马拉雅嵩草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">拉拉藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，多为音译字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(120)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">拗：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">羊角拗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，意为“弯曲”，因而不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">ao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">或</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> niu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(121)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">拧：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ning2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">拧条锦鸡儿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(122)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">杷：文读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pa2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枇杷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。但在普通话口语中常读为轻声。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(123)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">枇：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枇杷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(124)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">枥：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> li4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹅耳枥</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(125)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">沱：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tuo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莲沱兔儿风</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。莲沱为湖北西部地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(126)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">沽：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">省沽油</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(127)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">泞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ning4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">沼泞碱茅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ning2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(128)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">泾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jing1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">泾源紫堇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jing4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。泾源为宁夏县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(129)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">玡：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ya2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">琅玡榆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。琅玡（山）为安徽滁州山名。有人写作“琅琊榆”，是不符合地名规范的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(130)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">瓯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ou1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瓯柑</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(131)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">疝：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">治疝草、治疝星粟草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(132)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">的确景天</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">di2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(133)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">盂：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">盂兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(134)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">穹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qiong2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">浪穹耳蕨、穹窿薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(135)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">空：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">kong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">空棱芹、空竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> kong4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(136)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">竺：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天竺桂、天竺葵</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。“天竺”为印度古称。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(137)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">绉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhou4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绉面草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(138)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">肫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhun1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸡肫梅花草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(139)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">舍：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">舍季拉虎耳草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中为音译字，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">she4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> she3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。舍季拉为西藏东部山名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(140)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苓：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ling2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，常见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茯苓</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猪苓</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”二真菌名。在维管束植物中文名中用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">土茯苓</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苓菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”二名，后者为音译字（为其属名</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Jurinea </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">第二个音节的音译）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(141)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苔：在植物中文名中均读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> tai1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅用于“舌苔”一词，不用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(142)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苕：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">欧洲苕子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tiao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，苕子为豆科植物紫云英的别名。此字又读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> shao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“红苕”一词，则为番薯的地方俗名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(143)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苘：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qing3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苘麻、隔蒴苘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。注意不要误写为“茼”，误读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> tong2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(144)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苜：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苜蓿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，为古老的音译字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(145)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苨：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ni2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荠苨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(146)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">苳：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> dong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红茄苳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(147)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qie2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">番茄、颠茄</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jia1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅用于“雪茄”“茄克”等个别音译词，不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(148)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茑：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">niao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茑萝（松）</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(149)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">虮：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ji3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虮子草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(150)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">转：在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">转子莲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名中，按其字义，应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> zhuan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhuan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(151)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">轭：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">e4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牛轭草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(152)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">钗：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chai1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钗子股</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(153)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">阜：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">种阜草、阜平黄堇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> fu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(154)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鸢：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yuan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸢尾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名及其派生名如“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸢尾兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸢尾蒜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”等。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(155)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">冠：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">guan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸡冠花、瘤冠麻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> guan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(156)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">削：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xue1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">尖削箭竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，这里的“削”不能按普通话白读读成</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xiao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(157)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">哈：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，全部为音译字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">哈密棘豆、哈巴山马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音都不妥。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(158)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">奓：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zha4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">假奓包叶</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(159)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">奕：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> yi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">奕良龙胆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">奕武悬钩子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，均为人名用字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(160)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">将：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jiang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">将乐槭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。将乐是福建县名。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jiang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(161)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">峤：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qiao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">南峤滇竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。南峤为云南旧县名，位于今勐海县境内。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(162)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">彦：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萨彦柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。萨彦（岭）为山脉名，清为中俄界山，今属俄罗斯。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(163)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">指：此字今已统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，故“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">指甲兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中的“指”不宜再读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(164)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">挝：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wo1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，“老挝”为中南半岛国名。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhua1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(165)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">昴：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">昴山复叶耳蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">昴山蹄盖蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。昴山为浙江西南部山名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(166)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">枳：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枳、枳椇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(167)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">枹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枹栎、枹丝锥</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> fu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(168)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">柃：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ling2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柃木、柃叶山矾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(169)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">柊：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柊树、柊叶</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，也不能写为“苳”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(170)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">柘：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhe3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柘、柘藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(171)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">柞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zuo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柞木、柞槲栎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zha4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为地名特殊读音，不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(172)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">查：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">cha2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，均为音译字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">加查雪兔子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">布查早熟禾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">一般不作音译字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(173)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">柰：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">nai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，本指</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科苹果属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">花红</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">一类植物，但在《植物志》中仅用于姜科的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山柰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(174)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">柽：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">cheng1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柽柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。其它读音都是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(175)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">栀：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栀子、栀花素馨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(176)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">栅：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> zha4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栅枝垫柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此字有时会被误读成</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> shan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(177)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">栉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栉齿黄鹌菜、栉叶蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(178)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">栌：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄栌、栌菊木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(179)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">栎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">li4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栓皮栎、栎叶枇杷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yue4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为地名特殊读音，不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(180)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">毗：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> pi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毗黎勒</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毗邻雀麦</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(181)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">洮：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，地名用字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">洮河栒子、洮南灯芯草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(182)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">洱：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">er3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，地名用字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">普洱茶、洱源橐吾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(183)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">洼：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wa1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">洼皮冬青、洼瓣花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> wa4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(184)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">牯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> gu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牯岭凤仙花、牯岭野豌豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。“牯岭”为江西庐山小地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(185)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">珀：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">po4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">琥珀千里光、珀菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(186)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">珂：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ke1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">珂楠树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(187)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">癸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gui3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">丁癸草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”、“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">台东癸草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(188)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">看：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">kan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，只用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">看麦娘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> kan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">虽更常用，但不用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(189)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">禺：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禺毛茛</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(190)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">种：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> zhong3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">囊种草、斑种草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhong4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(191)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">秕：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">秕壳草、糠秕酸脚杆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(192)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">笃：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">du3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">粪箕笃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">笃斯越橘”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(193)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">籼：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">籼稻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(194)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">绕：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">rao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">缠绕挖耳草、缠绕党参</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> rao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(195)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">绛：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jiang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绛桃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绛车轴草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(196)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">胄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhou4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">胄叶线蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(197)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">背：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bei4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">银背菊、粉背蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bei1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(198)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">胫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jing4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">赤胫散</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(199)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茖：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ge2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茖葱</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(200)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茛：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> gen4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，注意不要误写为“莨”，也不要误读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> liang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">或</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">lang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(201)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茜：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> qian4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草、茜树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时仅为人名用字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(202)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茨：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ci2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茨藻、茨开乌头</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(203)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">土茯苓、茯蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(204)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茱：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，只出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茱萸</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(205)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茳：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jiang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，只出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茳芏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(206)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茼：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tong2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(207)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荁：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">huan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荁</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄花荁</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(208)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荏：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ren3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荏弱早熟禾、荏弱莠竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(209)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荛：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> rao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荛花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(210)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荜：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> bi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荜拔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">假荜拔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qiao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span
