style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(212)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荨：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qian2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荨麻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xun2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅用于“荨麻疹”，为《普通话异读词审音表》承认的俗读。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(213)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荩：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jin4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荩草、稗荩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(214)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sun1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">溪荪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(215)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yin1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荫生鼠尾草、喜荫草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yin4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(216)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荬：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mai3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小苦荬、苦荬菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(217)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荭：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hong2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">汉荭鱼腥草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此外，红蓼又名“荭草”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(218)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莛：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ting2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莛子藨、实莛葱</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(219)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">虻：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">meng2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虻眼</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(220)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">袅：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">niao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">纤袅凤仙花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(221)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">觉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jue2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">那觉小檗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">拉觉石杉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，均为藏语地名音译字。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">jiao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(222)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">贴：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tie1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">贴生石韦、贴毛苎麻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音都是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(223)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">重：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chong2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">重庆山茶、重羽菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhong4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(224)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">钤：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qian2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄钤勺兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(225)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">闾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> l</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">ü</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">庵闾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(226)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">骨：此字今已统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，故“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">狗骨头</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中的“骨”不宜再读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(227)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">倭：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wo1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">倭羽扇豆、倭竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(228)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">勐：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">meng3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">勐海槭、勐龙链珠藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。“勐”是云南西双版纳傣族地区旧行政区划单位，因此勐海、勐龙等都是云南南部地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(229)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">圃：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">滋圃报春</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。宋滋圃先生为我国植物分类学家。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(230)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">娑：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">suo1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">娑罗双</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名，为梵语音译，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(231)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">射：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">she4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">射毛悬竹、辐射龙胆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">射干</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的射笔者建议也读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> she4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，已见上文“多音字的整理”一段中的讨论。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(232)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">峪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">涝峪小檗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">涝峪薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。涝峪为陕西中部地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(233)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">㟖：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">long4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">㟖岗轮环藤、㟖岗马兜铃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(234)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">恶：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">e4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">恶味苘麻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">元谋恶味苘麻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(235)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">扇：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">扇蕨、扇叶槭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">shan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(236)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">旃：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蝎子旃那</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(237)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">晕：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> yun1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红晕杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">粉晕无心菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yun4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(238)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">栒：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xun2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栒子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(239)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">栘：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> yi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;color:#5B9BD5;">𣐿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> duo1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(240)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;">𣐿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;color:#5B9BD5;">𣐿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(241)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">栝：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gua1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栝楼</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(242)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">栲：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">kao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，《植物志》中仅使用一次，为单字植物名。其他带“栲”字的同属植物在《植物志》上均用“锥”字命名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(243)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">核：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">he2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">核桃、核果木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。普通话的白读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> hu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅在口语中出现。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(244)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">栾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">luan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栾树、朱栾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(245)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">桄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> guang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桄榔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(246)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">桉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">an1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓝桉、柠檬桉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(247)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">桔：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jie2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桔梗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名。此外，此字常用做“橘”的俗字。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(248)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">桕：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jiu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">乌桕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(249)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">桠：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ya1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">三桠苦、五桠果</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">ya4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(250)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">桤：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桤木、桤叶树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(251)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">桦：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hua4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">白桦、银桦</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">hua2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(252)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">桧：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> gui4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红桧、桧林毛茛</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> hui4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅用于人名（如秦桧）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(253)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">梣：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chen2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">欧梣、梣叶槭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">cen2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(254)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">浆：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jiang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">酸浆、酢浆草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jiang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(255)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">浚：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jun4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">德浚小檗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">德浚野丁香</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。俞德浚先生是我国著名植物采集家和植物分类学家。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(256)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">涞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> lai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">涞源鹅观草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。涞源为河北县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(257)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">狸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">li2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">狸藻、狸尾豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> li3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(258)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">珙：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gong3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">珙桐</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。珙桐是我国特产树种，国家一级保护植物。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(259)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">珥：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">er3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玫珥早熟禾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，为音译字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(260)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">痄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zha4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">痄腮树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(261)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">皋：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">皋月杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，此是日本汉字名，皋月为五月的别称。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(262)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">砧：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhen1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">砧草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(263)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">砻：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> long2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">雅砻雪胆、雅砻江楠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。雅砻江为四川西部水名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(264)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">秘：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">神秘果</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。有的《植物志》未收的外来植物名字中有南美国名“秘鲁”，此时“秘”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(265)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">笄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ji1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">笄石菖</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，此是日本汉字名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(266)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">紏：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tou3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牛紏吴萸</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛牛紏吴萸</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。这个字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中没有简化字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(267)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">绢：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">juan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绢毛石头花、绢蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> juan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(268)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">绥：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sui2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，全出现在地名中，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绥定苓菊、扶绥榕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(269)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">绦：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绦柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> tiao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(270)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">耙：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ba4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">犁耙柯</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pa2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(271)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">脂：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">胭脂花、补骨脂</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(272)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">脏：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">心脏形观音座莲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">心脏叶瓶尔小草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(273)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荵：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ren3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">花荵</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。此字常被误写为“葱”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(274)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荸荠、荸艾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(275)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荻：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">di2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">南荻、茅荻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(276)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荽：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sui1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天胡荽、芫荽</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。芫荽的“荽”在普通话口语中常读轻声。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(277)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莕：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xing4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莕菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(278)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莜：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> you2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莜麦</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。又如莜麦菜是莴苣的一个品种，近几年已成为常见蔬菜（《植物志》未收）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(279)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莠：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">you3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莠竹、莠狗尾草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(280)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莩：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莩草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名。读另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> piao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时，为“殍”的异体字，不用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(281)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> e2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莪术</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">广西莪术</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(282)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莳：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莳萝、莳萝蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> shi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(283)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莶：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豨莶</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(284)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">you2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">三花莸、莸叶醉鱼草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(285)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莼：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chun2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莼菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莼兰绣球</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(286)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蚬：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xian3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蚬壳花椒、蚬木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(287)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">调：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tiao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">调羹树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">调料九里香</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> diao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(288)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">豇：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jiang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豇豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(289)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">豺：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豺皮樟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> cai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(290)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">邕：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">邕宁香草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。邕宁为广西县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(291)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">都：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">du1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，除“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">都丽菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名为音译字外，均出现在地名中，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">武都棘豆、昌都韭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> dou1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(292)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">铎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">duo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">宝铎草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(293)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鸪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹧鸪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词（本为鸟名），如鹧鸪草、鹧鸪麻。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(294)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鸶：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">si1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹭鸶草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。鹭鸶本为鸟名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(295)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">乾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qian2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">乾宁乌头、乾精菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。读另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时，为干燥的“干”的繁体。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(296)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">偃：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">偃松、偃麦草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(297)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">假：此字在植物名中较常见，统读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jia3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jia4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(298)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">勒：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> le4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，多为音译字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">库尔勒沙拐枣、阿勒泰灯芯草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> lei1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(299)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">匙：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">匙叶草、匙叶甘松</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> shi</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（轻音）仅用于“钥匙”一词，不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(300)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">啮：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">nie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">啮蚀杜鹃、啮瓣景天</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(301)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">圈：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">quan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">圈药南星</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">卷圈野扁豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> juan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(302)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">崖：此字今统读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ya2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">ai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是旧读或地方俗读，在植物名中不宜使用。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(303)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">得：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">de2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">得荣小檗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">得荣</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">子梢</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。得荣为四川西部县名。其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(304)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">戛：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jia2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">戛氏马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">戛克氏马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">同戛乌头</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”三名。其他读音都是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(305)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">掖：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ye1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藏掖花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(306)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">斛：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石斛</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(307)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">旌：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jing1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">旌节马先蒿、旌节花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(308)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">桫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">suo1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桫椤、溪桫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(309)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">桲：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">榅桲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的“桲”文读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，但普通话口语读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> po</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（轻声），详见下文“科属中文名的普通话白读”一段。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(310)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">梓：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zi3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">梓、石梓、苦梓含笑</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(311)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">梵：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">梵净山盾蕨、梵天花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(312)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">梾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">梾木、沙梾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(313)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">涪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">涪陵续断</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">涪陵耳蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。涪陵现为重庆市的一个区。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(314)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">淆：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xiao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">混淆鳞毛蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(315)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">牻：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牻牛儿苗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(316)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">猄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jing1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄猄草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(317)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">琅：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">琅玡榆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(318)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">瓠：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瓠子”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瓠瓜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(319)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">㼎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马㼎儿、赤㼎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(320)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">畦：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">畦畔莎草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">畦畔飘拂草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(321)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">着：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhuo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">着色龙胆、着生杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(322)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">笹：为日本汉字，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">光笹竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此字又为“屉”的异体，可以读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ti4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(323)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">笼：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> long2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山一笼鸡、猪笼草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> long3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(324)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">筇：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qiong2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">筇竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(325)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">绯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> fei3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绯桃、绯红羊蹄甲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> fei1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(326)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">绰：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chuo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绰斯甲乌头</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。绰斯甲为四川西部地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(327)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">翎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ling2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红尾翎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(328)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">脬：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">球脬黄芪、马尿脬</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(329)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">脷：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> li4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">龙脷叶</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此字是粤方言的方言词，意为舌头。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(330)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菀：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> wan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫菀、乳菀</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(331)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菁：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jing1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">田菁、芜菁</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qing1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(332)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菅：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菅、毛菅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，注意与“管”不同。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(333)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菔：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> fu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">丛菔、菔根龙胆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(334)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菘：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">song1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菘蓝、臭菘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(335)[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">杭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菥：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(337)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菝：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ba2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菝葜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(338)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菟：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菟丝子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(339)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莨菪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(340)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菰：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菰、蛇菰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。菰的受黑粉菌感染膨大的茎做蔬菜时，叫茭白，茭音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">jiao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(341)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菵：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wang3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菵草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。《植物志》和许多其他专著上此字作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">/(</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">冂</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">@</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">又</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">)]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（括号表示先包围再上下），为错误字形。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(342)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(343)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">菽：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菽麻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(344)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">萁：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫萁、芒萁</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(345)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">萆：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绵萆薢</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山萆薢</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(346)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">萸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山茱萸、臭檀吴萸</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(347)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">䓫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">䓫莱乌头</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">䓫莱红门兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(348)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蛊：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蛊羊茅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蛊早熟禾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(349)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">酚：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fen1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">香酚草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(350)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">铛：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">铃铛</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，如铃铛刺、铃铛子。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> cheng1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(351)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">隅：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">察隅荨麻、门隅十大功劳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。察隅和门隅都是西藏东南部地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(352)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鸹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gua1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">老鸹铃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(353)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鸾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> luan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸾枝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，为榆叶梅一变种，常误作“蓝枝”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(354)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">麸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> fu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">麸杨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(355)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">厥：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jue2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">突厥益母草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">突厥蔷薇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。突厥为我国古代少数民族名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(356)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">厦：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> xia4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">厦门老鼠簕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">sha4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(357)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">喀：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ka1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，音译字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">日喀则蒿、喀什小檗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音都是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(358)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">喇：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">la3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">喇嘛蝇子草、喇叭瓶蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。“喇嘛”和“喇叭”中的“喇”都不能读成别的音。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(359)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">喙：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hui4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，是植物中文名中比较常见的一个字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">长喙葱、喙核桃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(360)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">婺：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> wu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">婺源凤仙花、婺源槭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。婺源为江西北部县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(361)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">孱：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">孱弱马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(362)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">嵌：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰嵌马蓝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中的“兰嵌”为台湾地名，此时“嵌”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">kan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qian4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(363)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">强：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qiang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">强竹、强壮杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(364)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">朝：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> chao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">朝鲜白头翁、水朝阳旋覆花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（按字义，其中的朝不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(365)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">棣：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> di4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唐棣、棣棠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(366)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">棯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">nian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为粤方言词，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">南美棯、黄花棯、地棯</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(367)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">椆：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chou2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">椆树桑寄生</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">椆琼楠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(368)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">椇：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ju3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枳椇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(369)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">椋：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">liang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红椋子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(370)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">椤：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> luo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桫椤、椤木石楠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(371)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">椪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">peng4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">椪柑</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(372)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">楮：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">楮</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">楮头红</span><span
