style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">斑点楮头红</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”三名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(373)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">渥：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">渥丹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(374)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">湄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mei2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">湄公鼠尾草、湄公木蓝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。湄公河是澜沧江在境外的名称。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(375)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">溲：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sou1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">溲疏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(376)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">瑯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">樟瑯乡南星</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。樟榔乡为湖北地名。此字《现汉》作为“琅”的异体字，但这仅限于琅玕、琳琅等非专有词，地名中的异体字有时不能轻易修改，故此处暂不更动。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(377)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">稃：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">沟稃草、光稃雀麦</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。这些名字中的“稃”是内稃或外稃的简称，这二者都是禾本科专用的花的描述术语。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(378)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">缙：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jin4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">缙云紫珠、缙云冬青</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(379)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">萩：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> qiu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">一叶萩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，为日本汉字名（日语中“萩”指豆科胡枝子属植物）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(380)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">萮：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山萮菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(381)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">萱：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xuan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萱草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(382)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">萹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> bian3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萹蓄</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(383)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">葎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> l</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">ü</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葎草、四叶葎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(384)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">葙：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xiang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">青葙</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(385)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">葜：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> qia1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菝葜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(386)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">葳：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wei1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫葳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百能葳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(387)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">葶：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ting2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葶苈</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(388)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蒌：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lou2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒌叶、蒌蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(389)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蒾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荚蒾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(390)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;">𫈰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qia4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;color:#5B9BD5;">𫈰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(391)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蜒：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蜿蜒杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(392)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">谟：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">望谟崖摩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">望谟毛蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，望谟为贵州县名。不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">mo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(393)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">跖：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸭跖草、鸦跖花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(394)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">酢：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">cu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">酢浆草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(395)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">铺：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">铺地秋海棠、铺散黄堇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(396)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">颏：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ke2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛颏马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛背毛颏马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(397)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">黍：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> shu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玉蜀黍、凤头黍</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。黍本身是禾本科植物稷的别名（一说和稷是两个不同的品种）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(398)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">嗉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">su4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸡嗉子榕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(399)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">塞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阿克塞蒿、边塞黄芪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(400)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">嵩：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">song1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">嵩草、嵩明省沽油</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(401)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">幌：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">huang3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">幌菊、幌伞枫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(402)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">数：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">四数木、五数苣苔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(403)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">楔：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xie1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">楔叶菊、楔苞楼梯草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">qi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">或</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(404)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">楝：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lian4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">川楝、非洲楝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jian3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(405)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">楞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">leng2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">拉卜楞杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。拉卜楞是甘肃西南部地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(406)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">楣：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mei2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">国楣复叶耳蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">国楣毛蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">国楣马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”三名。冯国楣先生是我国著名植物采集家。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(407)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">楤：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">song3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">楤木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> cong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(408)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">楷：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jie1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">青楷槭、楷叶梣</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。楷的本义是黄连木，作这个意义解时，不能读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">kai3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(409)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">楸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qiu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">灰楸、花楸树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(410)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">楹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ying2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">楹树、蓝花楹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(411)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">榅：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wen1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">榅桲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(412)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">榈：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> l</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">ü</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">棕榈、轴榈</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">l</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">ü</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(413)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">榉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ju3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">榉树、大果榉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(414)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">槌：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chui2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼓槌石斛、槌柱兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhui1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(415)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">槎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">cha2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">稻槎菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(416)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">溜：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> liu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">溜叶含笑</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> liu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(417)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">溥：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">个溥</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此名本义未详。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(418)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">溧：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> li4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">溧阳复叶耳蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，溧阳为江苏市名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(419)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">煜：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">学煜毛蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。侯学煜先生为我国著名生态学家。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(420)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">煲：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">沙煲暗罗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，原为粤方言词，今在普通话中也多有使用。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(421)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">瑙：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">nao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玛瑙石榴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玛瑙柑</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(422)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">畸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ji1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">畸形果鹤虱、畸裂盾蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(423)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">碇：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ding4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石碇佛甲草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。石碇为台湾北部地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(424)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">碚：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> bei4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“北碚槭”和“北碚榕”。北碚现为重庆市的一个区。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(425)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">稗：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> bai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如雀稗、稗荩。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(426)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">稞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ke1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">青稞</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藏青稞</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(427)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">窠：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ke1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蜂窠马兜铃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(428)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">筱：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xiao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">筱竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，为日本汉字名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(429)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">粳：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jing1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">粳稻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> geng3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(430)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">缝：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">feng4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">缝线海桐、石缝蝇子草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> feng2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(431)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">缢：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">缢筒列当</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">缢苞麻花头</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(432)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">腩：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">nan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鱼肚腩竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">nan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(433)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蒗：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">宁蒗龙胆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。宁蒗为云南西北部自治县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(434)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蒟：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ju3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山蒟、蒟蒻薯</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(435)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蒻：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ruo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒟蒻薯</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。蒟蒻本身为魔芋的别名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(436)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蒡：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牛蒡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(437)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蒺：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ji2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒺藜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(438)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蓂：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菥蓂</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的“蓂”音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> mi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ming2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(439)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蓊：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> weng3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">米面蓊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(440)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蓍：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓍、天山蓍</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。黄芪的“芪”，有时也被误写为“蓍”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(441)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蓑：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">suo1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小蓑衣藤、水蓑衣</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(442)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蓖：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓖麻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(443)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蓣：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薯蓣</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(444)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蓥：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ying2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">华蓥润楠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。华蓥为四川市名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(445)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蓪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓪梗花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(446)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">解：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jie3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">千解草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(447)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">谬：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> miu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">谬氏马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">刺冠谬氏马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">变形谬氏马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”三名，均为音译字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(448)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">貉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">he2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">貉藻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(449)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">赪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">cheng1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">赪桐</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">海南赪桐</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(450)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">锚：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">花锚、锚柱花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">miao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(451)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">韫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yun4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">韫珍金腰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。吴韫珍为我国著名植物分类学家。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(452)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">骞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">肇骞合耳菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。张肇骞为我国著名植物分类学家。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(453)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鹌：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">an1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄鹌菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(454)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">嘎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ga2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，音译字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">贡嘎乌头、萨嘎薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(455)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">嘛：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">喇嘛蝇子草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">嘛</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，普通话读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ma</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（轻声），其文读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ma2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(456)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">斡：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">斡花榕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(457)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">榧：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">fei3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">榧树、粗榧</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(458)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">榼：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ke1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">榼藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(459)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">槁：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">潺槁木姜子、茶槁楠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(460)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">槛：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苦槛蓝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中的“槛”应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> kan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jian4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(461)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">槟：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槟榔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> bing1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，但花红的别名槟子中的“槟”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bin1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(462)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">槠：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">米槠、甜槠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(463)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">槭：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">元宝槭、槭叶铁线莲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(464)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">模：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">酸模</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> mu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(465)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">獐：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">獐子松、獐牙菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(466)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">璃：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> li2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">琉璃草、琉璃繁缕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(467)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">瘩：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">刺疙瘩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芥菜疙瘩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瘩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，普通话读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> da</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（轻声），其文读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> da2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(468)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">箍：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gu1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">铁箍散</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(469)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">箐：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qing4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">箐姑草、箐边紫堇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(470)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">箕：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ji1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">簸箕柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">粪箕笃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(471)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">箣：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ce4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">箣柊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(472)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">箨：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tuo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">花箨唐竹、裸箨海竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(473)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">箬：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ruo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">箬竹、柳叶箬</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(474)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">綦：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">綦江假毛蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">綦江复叶耳蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。綦江为重庆县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(475)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">缫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">缫丝花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(476)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">膀：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，仅出现在“膀胱”一词中，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">膀胱果、膀胱蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bang3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(477)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蓼：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">liao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓼蓝、山蓼</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> liao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(478)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蓿：此字仅出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苜蓿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词中，普通话读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xu</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（轻声），文读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> su4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，详见下文“科属中文名的普通话白读”一段。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(479)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蔊：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">han4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔊菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(480)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蔓：此字在普通话中有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">man2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">man4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">wan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">三读。“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔓菁</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（芜菁的别名）的“蔓”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">man2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其他</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">man4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">wan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">都表示“细长而不能直立的茎”之意，但</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> wan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是白读，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">man4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是文读。依此，植物中文名中的蔓均应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">man4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(481)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蔗：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhe4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">甘蔗、蔗茅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhe2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(482)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蔹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lian3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">乌蔹莓、白蔹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(483)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蔺：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lin4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">花蔺、马蔺</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(484)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蔻：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> kou4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">肉豆蔻、小草蔻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(485)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蜞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蟛蜞菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(486)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蜿：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">wan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蜿蜒杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(487)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">螂：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">螳螂跌打</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(488)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">裴：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pei2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">裴氏马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，此处为音译字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(489)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">豨：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豨莶</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(490)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">銮：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">luan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹅銮鼻铁线莲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹅銮鼻大戟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹅銮鼻蔓榕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”三名。鹅銮鼻为台湾岛最南端。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(491)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">靼：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">da2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鞑靼滨藜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鞑靼狗娃花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> dan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(492)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">韶：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">韶子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> shao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(493)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">噎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ye1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">米扬噎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(494)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">噶：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ga2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，音译字，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">准噶尔大戟、贡噶翠雀花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(495)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">嶲：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">越嶲川木香</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(496)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">槲：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槲栎、槲寄生</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(497)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">槾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">man4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槾橘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(498)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">槿：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jin3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木槿、大麻槿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(499)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">樫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> jian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">樫木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(500)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">橄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">橄榄</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(501)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">潺：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山潺</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">潺槁木姜子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(502)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">澄：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> cheng2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">澄广花、澄迈秋海棠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> deng4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(503)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">澍：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">崇澍蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。钱崇澍先生是我国著名植物学家。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(504)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">澎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">peng2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">澎湖大豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> peng1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(505)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">熟：此字文读为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> shu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">shou2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为普通话白读，不宜用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(506)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">稷：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ji4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">稷、糠稷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(507)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">篌：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hou2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">篌竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">光箨篌竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(508)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;">𥯨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> si1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;color:#5B9BD5;">𥯨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">簩竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(509)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">缬：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xie2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">缬草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(510)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">羯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jie2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">羯布罗香</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(511)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">耧：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lou2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">耧斗菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。此名中的“耧斗”，今已通作“漏斗”，但鉴于耧漏同音不同调，且“耧斗菜”一名使用已经十分广泛，故不更改。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(512)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蕈：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xun4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，本为真菌担子菌的通称之一，维管束植物中文名中用于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蕈树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，指其木材可用于培养蕈类。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(513)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蕙：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hui4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蕙兰、峨眉春蕙</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(514)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蕤：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">rui2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蕤核</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(515)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蕲：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蕲艾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(516)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蕺：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ji2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蕺菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蕺叶秋海棠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(517)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">薁：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蘡薁</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(518)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">踯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">羊踯躅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(519)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">镒：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">征镒卫矛</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">征镒冬青</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。吴征镒先生是我国著名植物学家。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(520)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鞑：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">da2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鞑靼滨藜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鞑靼狗娃花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(521)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">髯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ran3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">髯毛凤仙花、髯管花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(522)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鲫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ji4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鲫鱼胆、鲫鱼藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(523)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鹞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹞落薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，鹞落坪为安徽西部地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(524)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">擂：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> lei2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">擂鼓簕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。其他读音均不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(525)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">樨：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木樨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(526)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">橉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lin4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">橉木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(527)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">橐：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tuo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">橐吾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(528)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">橼：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> yuan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">香橼</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(529)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">檎：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> qin2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">台湾林檎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">尖嘴林檎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(530)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">檠：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qing2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鬼灯檠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(531)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">檨：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">she1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山檨子、山檨叶泡花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">树。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(532)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">潞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">潞西柯、潞西胡颓子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。潞西为云南市名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(533)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">濑：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> lai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">濑水龙骨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(534)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">燕：植物中文名中的燕统读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，未见另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(535)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">甑：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> zeng4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">饭甑青冈</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">攀倒甑</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(536)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">瘿：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ying1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瘿花香茶菜、瘿椒树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span
