style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(537)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">穇：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">can3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">穇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">穇穗莎草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(538)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">篙：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">gao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">竹篙草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">撑篙竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(539)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蕗：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> lu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蕗蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(540)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蕹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">weng4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">水蕹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蕹菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(541)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蕻：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">hong2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">雪里蕻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(542)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">薏：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(543)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">薜：音</span><span zhe3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">双褶贝母兰、耳褶龙胆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(547)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">錾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">镘：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">man4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">镘瓣景天</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(549)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">镛：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yong1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">焕镛报春、焕镛粗叶木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。陈焕镛先生是我国著名植物分类学家。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(550)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">镞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">矢镞叶蟹甲草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(551)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">靛：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dian4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓝靛果、野靛棵</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(552)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">髭：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">髭脉槭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">髭脉桤叶树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">无髭毛建草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”三名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(553)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鹧：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> zhe4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“鹧鸪”一词（本为鸟名），如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹧鸪草、鹧鸪麻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(554)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">嶷：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> yi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">九嶷山连蕊茶</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，九嶷山为湖南南部山名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(555)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">懋：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">懋功荛花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，懋功是四川小金县的旧名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(556)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">擘：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(557)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">橿：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">jiang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山橿、橿子栎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(558)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">檗：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> bo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小檗、黄檗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(559)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">濞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">bi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">漾濞楼梯草、漾濞复叶耳蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。漾濞为云南西北部县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(560)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">篾：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">mie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">破篾黄竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(561)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">簕：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">le4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">簕竹、老鼠簕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(562)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">膻：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">羊红膻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(563)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">臌：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> gu3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">臌萼马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(564)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">薲：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">pin2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">麦薲草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(565)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">薷：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ru2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">香薷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(566)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">薸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">piao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大薸</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(567)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">薹：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">tai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薹草、芸薹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(568)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">藁：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> gao3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藁本</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(569)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">螫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">螫毛果</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">螫麻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。注意此字和“蜇”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(zhe1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">；</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">zhe2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不同。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(570)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蟀：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shuai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蟋蟀薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，但在普通话口语中常念轻声。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(571)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鹬：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鹬形马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(572)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">彝：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> yi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">彝良梅花草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。彝良为云南县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(573)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">檫：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">cha2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">檫木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(574)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">檵：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> ji4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">檵木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。此字没有简化字，有的人按“繼”简化为“继”类推，给“檵”也造了一个简化字，是不符合《简化字总表》的规范的，因为“继”不属于可以类推的简化字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(575)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">癞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lai4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">癞叶秋海棠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(576)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">瞿：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> qu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瞿麦</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(577)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">簩：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。此字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(578)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">簪：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玉簪、水玉簪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(579)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">繸：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sui4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(580)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葛藟葡萄</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”、“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓬藟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(588)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鼬：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼬瓣花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼬臭返顾马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(589)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">簸箕柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bo3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不见于植物中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(591)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">藿：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">huo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藿香、鹿藿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(592)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蘋：音</span><span style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(593)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鳔：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鱼鳔槐、鳔冠花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(594)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鳗：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黑鳗藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(595)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">麒：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">麒麟叶、木麒麟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(596)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">糯：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">nuo4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">糯米香、糯米椴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ru2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(597)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蘖：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">nie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">分蘖堇菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(598)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蘘：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">rang2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蘘荷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(599)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蘡：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">ying1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蘡薁</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。此字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(600)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">躅：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">zhu2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">羊踟躅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(601)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">馨：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xin1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">素馨花、馨香玉兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xing1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(602)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鳝：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">shan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鳝藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(603)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">黧：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">li2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黧蒴锥、山黧豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(604)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">夔：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> kui2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">夔州毛蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。夔州为重庆奉节县的旧称。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(605)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蘵：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> zhi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苦蘵</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛苦蘵</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(606)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">露：在植物中文名中统读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，另一读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> lou4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">仅用于口语，不宜用于植物名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(607)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">髓：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">sui3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">片髓灯芯草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">坚髓杜茎山</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sui2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(608)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鳢：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">li3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鳢肠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(609)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">麝：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">she4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛麝香、麝香阿魏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(610)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鹳：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> guan4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">老鹳草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(611)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">黐：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">chi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黐花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸟黐蛇菰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，为粤方言字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(612)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">欓：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">dang3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">簕欓花椒</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。此字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(613)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">虉：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">yi4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虉草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。此字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(614)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">觿：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">xi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">觿茅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(615)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">鬣：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">lie4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猪鬣凤尾蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鬣刺</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(616)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">圞：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> luan2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">土圞儿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一词。此字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字。</span></p><h2 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;">3.<span style="font-family:宋体;">科属中文名的普通话白读：</span></h2><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">上文已述，普通话中的白读主要体现在儿化、轻声和部分字音白读这三点上。其中，科属中文名中有文白读问题的字有“壳、爪”两字，上文“多音字的整理”一段已经进行了讨论，故下文从略，只讨论儿化和轻音这两种情况。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">所谓</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">儿化</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，是指做为某些名词、动词、形容词或副词等的后缀的“儿”失去其音节的独立性，而使前一字的韵母变成卷舌韵母的语音现象。由于植物中文名属于书面语系统，因此笔者建议，对于不带“儿”字的科属名，即使其名称中的某一部分在普通话口语中单独使用时常常儿化，在加上“科”或“属”字时也不宜再儿化。如桃、枣、豆瓣单用时常常儿化，说成桃儿、枣儿、豆瓣儿，但桃属、枣属、豆瓣菜属就不宜再念成桃儿属、枣儿属、豆瓣儿菜属。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这样一来，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">有儿化问题的科属名就只包括那些本身就带“儿”字的名字。这样的科属名一共有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">25</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如下（按音序排列）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">代儿茶属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dichrostachys</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:red;">不能儿化</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">粉条儿菜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Aletris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百合科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">勾儿茶属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Berchemia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼠李科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瓜儿豆属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cyamopsis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">孩儿参属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pseudostellaria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石竹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">孩儿草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rungia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石竹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄雀儿属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Priotropis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">金雀儿属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cytisus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">锦鸡儿属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Caragana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马㼎儿属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Zehneria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牻牛儿苗科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gentianaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牻牛儿苗属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Erodium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牻牛儿苗科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猫儿菊属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hypochaeris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猫儿屎属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Decaisnea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木通科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">帽儿瓜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mukia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绵枣儿属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Scilla</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百合科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒲儿根属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sinosenecio</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(18)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">雀儿豆属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Chesneya</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(19)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桃儿七属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sinopodophyllum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小檗科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(20)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">土圞儿属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Apios</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(21)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兔儿风属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ainsliaea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(22)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兔儿伞属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Syneilesis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(23)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">娃儿藤属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Tylophora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萝藦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(24)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小勾儿茶属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Berchemiella</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼠李科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(25)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸭儿芹属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cryptotaenia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伞形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">25</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个名字中，只有“代儿茶”因其意为“代替儿茶”（儿茶</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Acaciacatechu</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为豆科植物），其中的“儿”字是实义词，不能儿化；其他</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">24</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个名字中的“儿”都是名词后缀（勾儿茶、小勾儿茶二名和“儿茶”无干），因而在普通话口语中应该儿化。如牻牛儿苗，口语中应读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> mang2niur2miao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> mang2niu2er2miao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">或</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">mang2niu2er miao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（普通话口语中“儿”做后缀时必然儿化，不读单纯的轻声）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不过，有几个名字还需要再说明一下。“孩儿”一词，《现汉》有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">hai2er2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> hair2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">两种注音。前者为“父母称呼儿女或儿女对父母的自称（多见于早期白话）”，虽然《现汉》注明词性为名词，但多少有点人称代词的性质；后者则是普通的名词，意为“孩子”。“孩儿参”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和“孩儿草”中的“孩儿”显然是后一意义，故均应儿化，不能读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> hai2er2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">《现汉》收录了“家雀儿”（麻雀的别名）一词，注音为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">jia1qiaor3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，也即这里的“雀”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字在儿化时，还要白读（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">que4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为文读），但是这种读音只是北京土话。普通话虽然以北京方言为基础，但并不等同于北京方言，所以并未对北京方言中所有的词和音兼收并蓄，像“雀”的这种白读，就应只局限用于这一个词，而不能推而广之。因此，“黄雀儿”“金雀儿”“雀儿豆”中的“雀儿”虽然应儿化，但要读成</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> quer4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不宜读成</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qiaor3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">普通话中的轻声有三种情况，一种是某些助词、后缀只有轻声的读音，如“地”“了”“吗”“啊”“子”“头”等（但这些字往往是多音多义字，除做助词、后缀外，在表示其他意义时，通常都有声调），一种是某些只用来记写多音节语素（多半是双音节语素）的最末音节的字只有轻声的读音，如苜蓿、榅桲等（这些字原本是有文读的，只是在普通话口语中不用而已），一种是某些字通常不轻读，但出现在某些多音节词（多半也是双音节词）的最末时，习惯要轻读，如慈姑、芫荽等。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">在植物中文名中，“子”和“头”是两个较常见的名词后缀，但这两个字又可作实义词，而且在植物中文名更多见。具体来说，在含“子”的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">11</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个科名、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">104</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个属名中，就有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">9</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个科名、</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">63</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">个属名中的“子”是实义词，不能轻读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">裸子蕨、使君子、九子母、莲子草、棋子豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。这些做实义词的“子”多是“种子”或“孢子”的简称（有时实际指的是果实）。大部分这样的做实义词的“子”是易于识别的，但也有一些名字中的“子”可能容易被误当成名词后缀，而在口语误读为轻声，兹举十例辨析：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">诃子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Terminalia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">使君子科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：此名为音译，“子”是音译字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">乱子草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Muhlenbergia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：“乱子”指其颖果上宿存的芒长而相互交织，看上去比较凌乱，不是口语中的“祸事；纠纷”之意。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菟丝子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cuscuta</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">旋花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：此名本为中药名，因其原植物的药用部分为种子，故名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸦胆子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brucea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苦木科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：同上，药用部分为种子，苦如鸦胆，故名。“胆子”在这里不是“胆量”之意。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天蓬子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Atropanthe</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：该属植物的花萼在果期宿存，罩于果外，似斗蓬，故名。“子”在这里实际上指的是其果实。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">珠子木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Phyllanthodendron</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大戟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：“珠子”指其果实（不是种子）近球形，像珍珠，不是“珍珠”之意。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">麦珠子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Alphitonia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼠李科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：同上，“珠子”指其果实（不是种子）为球形。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">韶子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Nephelium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">无患子科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：韶子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> N. chryseum </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的种子的假种皮可食，韶为“美好”之意，是赞美之辞。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">假韶子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Paranephelium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">无患子科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：为上名的衍生名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瘤子草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Nelsonia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">爵床科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），“瘤子”指其种子上有瘤状小突起。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">其余“子”做名词后缀的两个科名是：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山柚子科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Opiliaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">眼子菜科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Potamogetonaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">；属名有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">41</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个，如下（按音序排列，个别名称略作说明）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豹子花属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Nomocharis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百合科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茶藨子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ribes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虎耳草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钗子股属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Luisia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），“钗子”是旧时妇女的一种头饰，由两股簪子合成，在此名中形容该属植物叶为细长圆柱形，似簪子；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大叶子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Astilboides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虎耳草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">拂子茅属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Calamagrostis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），“拂子”即拂尘，状其多柔毛的花序似拂尘；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葛缕子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Carum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伞形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">盒子草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Actinostemma</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">胡枝子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lespedeza</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虎榛子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ostryopsis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桦木科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">金叶子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Craibiodendron</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">子梢属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Campylotropis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">帘子藤属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pottsia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">夹竹桃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），《植物志》载：帘子藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> P. laxiflora</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">“果实长而细，且数量多，下垂有如门帘”，故广西十万大山居民称之为“帘子藤”；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">铃子香属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Chelonopsis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蚂蚱腿子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Myripnois</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒙蒿子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Anaxagorea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">番荔枝科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木姜子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Litsea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">樟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">奶子藤属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bousigonia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">夹竹桃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），指该属植物茎有白色乳汁；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(18)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">纽子花属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Vallaris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">夹竹桃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），“纽子”即纽扣；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(19)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山茄子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brachybotrys</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(20)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山檨子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Buchanania</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">漆树科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(21)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山柚子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Opilia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山柚子科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(22)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蛇婆子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Waltheria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">梧桐科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），“婆子”方言为“妻子”之意，蛇婆子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> W.indica </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为蔓状半灌木，常在地面匍匐生长，故有此名；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(23)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">酸藤子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Embelia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫金牛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(24)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">梭子果属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eberhardtia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山榄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），指其果实形似梭子；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(25)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">铁筷子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Helleborus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(26)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莛子藨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Triosteum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">忍冬科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莛子藨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">T.pinnatifidum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">在开花时，茎顶生分枝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对，高达</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">60</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">厘米，“莛子”指的就是这</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对分枝；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(27)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蚊子草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Filipendula</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(28)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">响盒子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hura</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大戟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(29)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蝎子草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Girardinia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荨麻科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(30)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">新木姜子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Neolitsea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">樟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(31)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">悬钩子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rubus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(32)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栒子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cotoneaster</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(33)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">眼子菜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Potamogeton</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">眼子菜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(34)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">羊胡子草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eriophorum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(35)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">椰子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cocos</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">棕榈科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(36)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">叶子花属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bougainvillea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫茉莉科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(37)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蝇子草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Silene</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石竹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(38)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栀子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gardenia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(39)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栀子皮属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Itoa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大风子科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(40)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">竹叶子属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Streptolirion</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸭跖草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(41)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">砖子苗属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mariscus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），其坚果三棱形，形不似砖，故“子”不太可能是指果实，但有可能是粤方言或闽方言字“仔”的误写。在未考证清楚之前，权作名词后缀看待。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">在有“头”字的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">29</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">个属名中，更是有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">28</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">个都不能轻读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，只有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石头花属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gypsophila</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石竹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）一名中的“头”应</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">轻读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓝刺头属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Echinops</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“头”，有人也轻读，这属于土话，不宜作为规范。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">上述轻声的第二种情况是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">某些只用来记写多音节语素（多半是双音节语素）的最末音节的字只有轻声的读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。这类字在科中文名中不存在，在属中文名中，也只有三个字如此，即</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（白读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> xu </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">轻声，文读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> su4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（白读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> po </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">轻声，文读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">卜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（繁体为“蔔”，白读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bo</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">轻声，文读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bo2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。需要注意的是，前二个字的文白读声母也是不同的。含有这三个字的属中文名有以下</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">6</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苜蓿属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Medicago</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> </span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">墨苜蓿属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Richardia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">榅桲属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cydonia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萝卜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Raphanus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">胡萝卜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Daucus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伞形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> </span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">树萝卜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Agapetes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">至于某些多音节词的最末音节读轻声的情况，则无明显规律可言，只能是约定俗成，而且有的词轻读不轻读均可，不过一般来说，这种需要轻读最末音节的多音节词都是在日常生活中比较常见的词，所以数目并不多。现根据《现汉》的注音，将科属中文名中的这种情况分析如下。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">一般应轻读最末音节的词有：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">棒槌：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">棒槌瓜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Neoalsomitra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">扁担：见于</span><span
