style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">扁担杆属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Grewia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">椴树科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">薄荷：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薄荷属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mentha </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">美国薄荷属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Monarda</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">慈姑：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">慈姑属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sagittaria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">泽泻科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山慈姑属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Iphigenia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百合科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">豆腐：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆腐柴属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Premna</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马鞭草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">风筝：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">风筝果属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hiptage</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">金虎尾科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">甘蔗：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">甘蔗属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Saccharum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">高粱：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">高粱属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sorghum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">核桃：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">喙核桃属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Annamocarya</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山核桃属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Carya</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">胡桃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。但胡桃的“桃”字不轻读。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和尚：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">和尚菜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Adenocaulon</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">葫芦：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lagenariaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lagenaria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦茶属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Tadehagi</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦树属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Crescentia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫葳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）四名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">口袋：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">米口袋属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gueldenstaedtia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">铃铛：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">铃铛刺属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Halimodendron</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">骆驼：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">骆驼刺属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Alhagi</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">骆驼蓬属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Peganum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒺藜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">玫瑰：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玫瑰木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhodamnia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桃金娘科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玫瑰树属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ochrosia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">夹竹桃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">牡丹：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野牡丹科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Melastomataceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荷包牡丹属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dicentra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">罂粟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">牡丹草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gymnospermium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小檗科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藤牡丹属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Diplectria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野牡丹属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Melastoma</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野牡丹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）五名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">木樨：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木樨科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oleaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木樨草科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Resedaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">草木樨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Melilotus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木樨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Osmanthus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木樨榄属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Olea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木樨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木樨草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Reseda</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木樨草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）六名。但</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">川樨草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oligomeris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木樨草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“樨”字不轻读。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(18)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芍药：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芍药属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Paeonia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，《植物志》上此属归于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。若独立为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芍药科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Paeoniaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，则这一科名中的“药”字也应轻读。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(19)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">石榴：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石榴科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Punicaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">番石榴属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Psidium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桃金娘科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山石榴属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Catunaregam</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石榴属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Punica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">石榴科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）四名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(20)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芫荽：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山芫荽属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cotula</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芫荽属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Coriandrum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伞形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二种。但胡荽的“荽”字不轻读。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(21)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">芝麻：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野芝麻属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lamium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">假野芝麻属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Paralamium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小野芝麻属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Galeobdolon</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">异野芝麻属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Heterolamium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（四者均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山芝麻属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Helicteres</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">梧桐科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芝麻菜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eruca</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）六种。但胡麻的“麻”字不轻读。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(22)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">叠字的情况。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">婆婆纳属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Veronica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">假婆婆纳属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Stimpsonia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">报春花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">香科科属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Teucrium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">花花柴属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Karelinia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">盐爪爪属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Kalidium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）五名中的第二个叠字应轻读。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">可轻读可不轻读（一般轻读）最末音节的词有：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荸荠：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荸荠属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Heleocharis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">茉莉：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">刺茉莉科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Salvadoraceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫茉莉科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Nyctaginaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">刺茉莉属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Azima</span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">刺茉莉科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茉莉果属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Parastyrax</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山茉莉属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Huodendron</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">安息香科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山茉莉芹属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oreomyrrhis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伞形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山紫茉莉属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oxybaphus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫茉莉属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mirabilis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫茉莉科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）八名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">冬瓜：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">冬瓜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Benincasa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">荷包：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荷包藤属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Adlumia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荷包牡丹属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dicentra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">罂粟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。对后者，因“包”和“丹”若均轻读，则听上去比较别扭，故其中的“包”字习惯不轻读。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">黄瓜：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄瓜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cucumis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和黄瓜菜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Paraixeris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">南瓜：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">南瓜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cucurbita</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">枇杷：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枇杷属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eriobotrya</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">葡萄：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葡萄科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Vitaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葡萄属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Vitis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蛇葡萄属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ampelopsis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葡萄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）三名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">尿泡：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马尿泡属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Przewalskia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莴苣：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山莴苣属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lagedium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莴苣属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lactuca</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">细莴苣属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Stenoseris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（三者均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）三名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蜈蚣：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">水蜈蚣属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Kyllinga</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蜈蚣草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eremochloa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">西瓜：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">西瓜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Citrullus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">樱桃：见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">番樱桃属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eugenia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桃金娘科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">最后要说明的是，某些在北京方言中轻读的词，在普通话中不轻读。如“茴香”和“檵木”，北京方言习惯轻读第二字，但《现汉》注音为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> hui2xiang1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ji4mu4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。总之，只要是上述未列举的名称，一般就不宜再轻读。</span></p><h2 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;"><span style="font-family:宋体;">附：科属中文名中的同音名称</span></h2><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和重名不同，同音名称不属于必须纠正的情况，因为语音总是在不断演变中的，过去的同音，将来可能变得不同音，过去的不同音，将来也可能变得同音；而且在普通话中的同音，到方言中就不一定同音，反之亦然。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">但是，找出植物中文名中的同音名称，还是有意义的。比如对于等级较高、数目较少的类群，应尽量做到无同音名称。像《植物志》科中文名中</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桤叶树科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Clethraceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">七叶树科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hippocastanaceae </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">同音（这也是科中文名中唯一一对同音名称），有时就会引起混淆。如果前者使用别名“山柳科”作为中文正名，就可以避免这种混淆（虽然这样一来，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杨柳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山柳</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Salix pseudotangii </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">也要改名，但这个代价显然是值得的）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">又如《植物志》上的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瓶尔小草科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ophioglossaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，有的蕨类学家以名字太长、体现不出是蕨类植物为由，建议改为“箭蕨科”，但这样就与</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">剑蕨科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Loxogrammaceae </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">同音，因此笔者认为是不合适的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">《植物志》属中文名中，也有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">17</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">对同音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，有的还是同一科中的两个属同音。下面就把这</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">17</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对属名列在下面（按音序排列），作为本文的结束。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">带唇兰属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Tainia </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">袋唇兰属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hylophila</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">风箱树属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cephalanthus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">枫香树属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Liquidambar</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">金缕梅科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">核果木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Drypetes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大戟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">合果木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Paramichelia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荠属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Capsella</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓟属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cirsium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蕉木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oncodostigma</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">番荔枝科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">胶木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Palaquium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山榄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">节毛蕨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lastreopsis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">叉蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">睫毛蕨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pleurosoriopsis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">睫毛蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">金唇兰属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Chrysoglossum </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">巾唇兰属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pennilabium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Chenopodium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">梨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pyrus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">栗属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木兰属</span><em><span
